$CATEGORY: $course$ / Examples / For_Loops_Printing1

::For Loops Printing Level 1 #000::
What is the following output of the code?
<pre>for (int a = 4; a < 6; a = a + 1)
\{
	cout << a << ' ';
\}
</pre>	{
	=4 5 
	~5 
	~5 6 
	~4 
	~4 5 6 
	}

<pre>for (int d = 70; d < 98; d = d + 10)
\{
	cout << d << ' ';
\}
</pre>	{
	=70 80 90 
	~80 90 
	~80 90 100 
	~70 80 
	~70 80 90 100 
	}

<pre>for (int h = 40; h < 70; h = h + 10)
\{
	cout << h << ' ';
\}
</pre>	{
	=40 50 60 
	~50 60 
	~50 60 70 
	~40 50 
	~40 50 60 70 
	}

	cout << d << ' ';
\}
</pre>	{
	=8 4 
	~4 
	~4 2 
	~8 
	~8 4 2 
	}

	~3 30 300 
	}
